giveaway! We have so many projects that are being developed for you guys to help keep you safe when buying and selling as well as help you buy or sell a gun quickly, safely and easily from your mobile device! Make sure you register so you can be the first to hear about the launch of our upcoming game changing technology that will change the way the whole country buys and sells guns forever.<br> <br> Make sure to list your firearms for sale on the page and help us grow! Your gun is automatically posted on over 10 different social media networks to get maximum exposure. <br> <br> He is an NRA certified instructor and teaches firearm training classes.</p> </div> comment-bubble"><a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/fn-57/#respond" class="bubble cp-fixed-color">0</a></div> <h3 class="loop"><a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/fn-57/" title="FN 57 MKII Review – Buy FN 57 Now">FN 57 MKII Review – Buy FN 57 Now</a></h3> <p class="meta dotted"><span class="dashicons-before user"><a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/author/matt-adika/" title="Posts by Matt Adika" rel="author">Matt Adika</a></span> <span class="dashicons-before folderb"><a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/category/firearms-blog/" rel="category tag">Firearms Blog</a></span> <span class="dashicons-before clock"><span>March 24, 2015</span></span></p> <div class="entry-content"> <img width="150" height="99" src="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/DSC_1439.jpg?fit=150%2C99" class="attachment-blog-thumbnail size-blog-thumbnail wp-post-image" alt="fn 57" srcset="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/DSC_1439.jpg?w=2464 2464w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/DSC_1439.jpg?resize=50%2C33 50w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/DSC_1439.jpg?resize=200%2C132 200w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/DSC_1439.jpg?resize=500%2C331 500w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/DSC_1439.jpg?resize=100%2C66 100w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/DSC_1439.jpg?resize=150%2C99 150w" sizes="(max-width: 150px) 100vw, 150px"> <h2 style="text-align: justify;"></h2> <h2 style="text-align: justify;">FN 57 was tested and <strong>shot</strong>&nbsp;with SS190, SS192, SS195, SS197, SS198LF and American Eagle ammo against a 15 pound Ham, a frozen turkey and AR500 Level III hard body armor.</h2> <p style="text-align: center;">Florida Gun Classifieds is proud to have just launched a brand new website that sells only FN 57 and <a href="http://fnamerica.com" target="_blank">FNH USA</a> firearms!</p> <p style="text-align: center; font-size: 130%;">VISIT TO ENTER TO WIN A FN 57:</p> <p style="text-align: center; font-size: 200%;"><a href="http://fn57sale.com" target="_blank">www.FN57SALE.com</a></p> <p style="text-align: center;">Best prices and selection on all FNH USA FIREARMS!</p> <p><a class="cboxElement" href="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/DSC_1439.jpg" data-rel="colorbox"><img class="aligncenter wp-image-3067 size-large" src="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/DSC_1439.jpg?resize=500%2C331" alt="fn 57" srcset="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/DSC_1439.jpg?resize=500%2C331 500w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/DSC_1439.jpg?resize=50%2C33 50w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/DSC_1439.jpg?resize=200%2C132 200w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/DSC_1439.jpg?resize=100%2C66 100w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/DSC_1439.jpg?resize=150%2C99 150w" sizes="(max-width: 500px) 100vw, 500px" data-recalc-dims="1"></a></p> <p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>FN 57&nbsp;MK2 Review</strong>&nbsp;was one of my favorite videos to shoot. I love the Five seveN Mk2. I believe it is the best pistol hands down to any other on the market. It allows the shooter a variety of different ammunition for different practical purposes. Before we begin, lets lay out the different ammo used in the shoot and explain what each is designed to do.</p> <ul> <li>American Eagle .40 grain – Used for cheap target practice</li> <li>SS197SR 40 grain – Sporting Round used for target practice or to hunt varmint</li> <li>SS196 – 40 grain – Vmax bullet that was replaced with the SS197SR</li> <li>SS195 – 27 grain – hollow point that is used for various purposes.</li> <li>SS192 – 28 grain hollow point (banned in 2004 for is potential armor penetrating capabilities.</li> <li>SS198LF – 27 grain hollow point (used by LEO/MILITARY for its devastating effects on soft tissue. The projectile is designed on impact to tumble causing massive destruction to soft tissue as the video will show.</li> <li>SS190 – 28 grain steel core black tip designed as Armor Penetrating Ammunition.</li> </ul> <p><a class="cboxElement" href="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/ammo-bullets.jpg" data-rel="colorbox"><img class="aligncenter wp-image-3072 size-medium" src="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/ammo-bullets.jpg?resize=172%2C150" sizes="(max-width: 172px) 100vw, 172px" srcset="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/ammo-bullets.jpg?resize=172%2C150 172w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/ammo-bullets.jpg?w=500 500w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/ammo-bullets.jpg?resize=150%2C131 150w" alt="fn-five-seven-mk2-review" width="172" height="150"></a></p> <p style="text-align: justify;">In my&nbsp;<strong>FN 57&nbsp;MK2 Review</strong> we shot each of these rounds at various objects. The first being a 15 pound ham. You get to see how the pistol shoots first, then we show you a full speed closeup of the Ham being shot, then the slow mo footage where you can see which rounds do the most damage.</p> <p><img class=" wp-image-3069 alignleft" src="http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/DSC_1443.jpg?resize=426%2C282" sizes="(max-width: 426px) 100vw, 426px" alt="fn-five-seven-mk2-review" width="207" height="280"></a></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p style="text-align: justify;">In the second shoot of the&nbsp;<strong>FN 57&nbsp;MK2 Review</strong> we shoot the same sequence of rounds at a frozen turkey which does not exit the turkey. Didn’t expect it to it was pretty much a solid rock a ice.</p> <p style="text-align: justify;">In the third shoot of the&nbsp;<strong>FN 57&nbsp;MK2 Review</strong> we shoot each of the rounds again at&nbsp;<strong>AR500</strong> level III hard body armor to see what the sequence of rounds would do, and then shoot four SS190 AP Black Tips at the plate. The AR500 Armor is designed to withstand a shot from a .308, so we weren’t expecting much.</p> <p><a class="cboxElement" href="http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/DSC_1449.jpg" data-rel="colorbox"><img class="aligncenter wp-image-3071 size-large" href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/liberty-civil-defense-ammo/#comments" class="bubble cp-fixed-color">4</a></div> <h3 class="loop"><a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/liberty-civil-defense-ammo/" title="Liberty Civil Defense Ammo For Sale">Liberty Civil Defense Ammo For Sale</a></h3> <p class="meta dotted"><span class="dashicons-before user"><a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/author/matt-adika/" title="Posts by Matt Adika" rel="author">Matt Adika</a></span> <span class="dashicons-before folderb"><a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/category/firearms-blog/" rel="category tag">Firearms Blog</a></span> <span class="dashicons-before clock"><span>March 7, 2015</span></span></p> <div class="entry-content"> <img width="150" height="52" src="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/civildefense1.jpg?fit=150%2C52" class="attachment-blog-thumbnail size-blog-thumbnail wp-post-image" alt="liberty-civil-defense-ammo" srcset="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/civildefense1.jpg?w=550 550w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/civildefense1.jpg?resize=200%2C70 200w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/civildefense1.jpg?resize=500%2C175 500w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/civildefense1.jpg?resize=100%2C35 100w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/civildefense1.jpg?resize=150%2C52 150w" sizes="(max-width: 150px) 100vw, 150px"> <h1 style="font-size: 250%; text-align: center;"><strong>Liberty Civil Defense Ammo&nbsp;For Sale</strong></h1> <p style="text-align: center;"><a href="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/civildefense1.jpg" data-rel="colorbox"><img class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-2720" src="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/civildefense1.jpg?resize=500%2C175" alt="liberty-civil-defense-ammo" srcset="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/civildefense1.jpg?w=550 550w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/civildefense1.jpg?resize=200%2C70 200w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/civildefense1.jpg?resize=500%2C175 500w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/civildefense1.jpg?resize=100%2C35 100w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/civildefense1.jpg?resize=150%2C52 150w" sizes="(max-width: 550px) 100vw, 550px" data-recalc-dims="1"></a></p> <h2 style="text-align: center; font-size: 150%;">Liberty Civil Defense Ammo Review</h2> <p><iframe src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/rCtpFH3oX48" width="560" height="315" frameborder="0" allowfullscreen="allowfullscreen"></iframe></p> <h3 style="text-align: center; font-size: 150%;">Whats up with this aluminum hollow point ammo I keep hearing about?</h3> <p style="font-size: 100%; text-align: left;">When I first heard about Liberty Civil Defense ammunition, I was one of the first to dismiss this new light aluminum ammunition as another marketing gimmick, but the ammo intrigued me so I decided to do some research and see what this ammo was all about. I immediately noticed how light the bullets when compared to the other personal defense ammunition on the market. 50 grain for a 9mm bullet? What were they thinking! But then after reading further, I saw how fast this projectile traveled. 2000 feet per second! I was impressed. My Five seveN ammunition travels about 2300 feet per second out of a 5” barrel, and its a 27 grain bullet with a rifle style cartridge. I began thinking back to high school physics which reminded me, MASS x VELOCITY = MOMENTUM. So a lighter bullet traveling twice as fast as a heavier bullet should have a similar total energy disbursement and therefore similar results right? This is what I was determined to find out.</p> <h3 style="text-align: center; font-size: 150%;">What is Liberty Civil Defense Ammo?</h3> <p style="font-size: 100%; text-align: left;">Civil Defense is the company’s line of civilian ammunition. It is designed to quickly incapacitate a violent attacker by causing massive hemorrhaging, while still allowing for enough penetration to reach vital organs and crush bones. These ammunition cartridges use a monolithic copper bullet that is lighter a normal bullet of the same caliber. These bullets&nbsp;achieve extremely high velocities from standard handguns. Unlike some of Liberty’s predecessors that have been offered in the past from companies like Corbon, Liberty’s bullets use a deep hollow point design&nbsp;which upon impact of soft tissue, forces the bullet to fragment causing massive damage.</p> <p style="font-size: 100%; text-align: left;"><a href="http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/trifold21.jpg" data-rel="colorbox"><img class="aligncenter wp-image-2722 size-full" src="http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/trifold21.jpg?resize=500%2C377" alt="liberty-civil-defense-ammo" srcset="http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/trifold21.jpg?w=580 580w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/trifold21.jpg?resize=200%2C150 200w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/trifold21.jpg?resize=500%2C376 500w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/trifold21.jpg?resize=100%2C75 100w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/trifold21.jpg?resize=150%2C113 150w" sizes="(max-width: 580px) 100vw, 580px" data-recalc-dims="1"></a><a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/Deep-Hollowpoint-Photo1.jpg"><br> </a></p> <p style="font-size: 100%; text-align: left;">I read a few different articles around the internet and each article had a different opinion on the effectiveness of this ammunition, but none of these geniuses actually did any real world testing with the ammunition. They just assumed that because of the lighter weight, the bullet would have a hard time penetrating barriers such as thick denim, glass, car doors and other dense materials. “you need to have 18 inches of penetration according to the experts” I kept hearing. 18”? I don’t know about you, but shoot me with a bullet that penetrates 18” and the person who was unlucky to be behind me is also going to end up with a hole in them as well. So after hours of research, I was no closer to finding out the answer to my question. “Is this ammo any good?” So instead of waste anymore time with wanna be internet ballistics guru’s, I decided to pack up my toys, grab some of the most common barriers one would encounter in a real world scenario, and head out to the Florida Everglades to set up my own test of this super light super fast ammunition. I was finally going to actually figure out whats really going on with this Liberty Civil Defense Ammo.</p> <h5 style="font-size: 150%; text-align: center;">To prepare for the shoot I gathered the following barriers to test the ammo on:</h5> <ol> <li>3/4” Sheet Rock to simulate a home wall</li> <li>1/2” Sheet Rock again to simulate a wall or similar barrier</li> <li>1/4” Particle board &nbsp;which could simulate a table or some light barrier</li> <li>A door from a Volkswagen &nbsp;Jetta</li> <li>Automobile glass</li> <li>Thin sheet metal to put behind the barriers so we could see what the exit holes looked like.</li> </ol> <p><img class="size-full wp-image-2717 alignnone aligncenter" src="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/setup-door.jpg?resize=418%2C313" alt="liberty-civil-defense-ammo" srcset="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/setup-door.jpg?w=418 418w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/setup-door.jpg?resize=200%2C150 200w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/setup-door.jpg?resize=100%2C74 100w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/setup-door.jpg?resize=150%2C112 150w" sizes="(max-width: 418px) 100vw, 418px" data-recalc-dims="1"></p> <p>We also wanted to test the most common calibers that the everyday person would be carrying in their firearm, so we brought four different firearms that each shot a different caliber.</p> <ol> <li>Keltec .380 1.875” barrel with&nbsp;Liberty .380 50 grain bullet at 1500 fps</li> <li>Beretta Nano 9mm 3” barrel&nbsp;with&nbsp;Liberty 9mm 50 grain bullet at 2000 fps</li> <li>Sig Sauer P229 .40 S&amp;W 4” barrel&nbsp;with Liberty .40cal 60 grain bullet at 2000 fps</li> <li>FN FNX .45 Tactical with an Advanced Armament Shepard suppressor &nbsp;with Liberty .45acp 78 grain bullet at 1900 fps.</li> </ol> <p><img class="aligncenter wp-image-2715 size-large" src="http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/guns.jpg?resize=500%2C172" alt="liberty-civil-defense-ammo" srcset="http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/guns.jpg?resize=500%2C172 500w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/guns.jpg?resize=200%2C68 200w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/guns.jpg?resize=100%2C34 100w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/guns.jpg?resize=150%2C51 150w" sizes="(max-width: 500px) 100vw, 500px" data-recalc-dims="1"></p> <p style="font-size: 100%; text-align: left;">For some added fun I cooked up some ballistic gel in my kitchen and it turned out pretty cool. The gel was created to mimic a human torso. We added a heart with strawberry syrup in the middle, some wax ribs, two kidneys and some lungs all to see what this liberty ammo would do to what organs. The ballistic gel I created we later found out was to small to really be of any value to the test. The size of the gel was too small to really use behind the barrier so we could try and capture what would happen to the bullet after it went through a barrier. Due to my lack of experience with ballistics gel and the correct sizes needed for experiments like this, we quickly realized that my 14” x 9” baking pan mold was no where near the amount needed to be large enough to make the gel effective in taking hits and being able to then use it for accurate readings, but we put that behind the barrier anyway to see what would happen for my own amusement. For our follow up video I plan on obtaining a large block of actual ballistic gel.</p> <p style="font-size: 100%; text-align: left;"><a href="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/gel.png" data-rel="colorbox"><img class="aligncenter size-large wp-image-2708" src="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/gel.png?resize=500%2C211" alt="liberty-civil-defense-ammunition" srcset="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/gel.png?resize=500%2C211 500w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/gel.png?resize=200%2C84 200w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/gel.png?resize=100%2C42 100w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/gel.png?resize=150%2C63 150w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/gel.png?w=597 597w" sizes="(max-width: 500px) 100vw, 500px" data-recalc-dims="1"></a></p> <p style="font-size: 100%; text-align: left;">We all agreed that the toughest barrier we brought with us would be the car door, so we set that up first with one 1/2” sheet rock layer about 1 foot behind the car door, and then behind that we set up a few more layers of the 3/4” sheet rock about 1 foot apart from each other, so we could see how much penetration would occur once it hit that hard first barrier, the second dry wall barrier and then if it continued through, how far it would actually travel and the effects. We figured because of the weight of the bullet, a few barriers should be more than enough and we would be able to capture some of the projectiles from the dry wall boards in the back. Guess what? <strong>We were completely WRONG!</strong> The ammo was so effective in penetrating, that it actually went right through every barrier we put up, which really took us all by surprise. After reading those articles online that this ammo might have a hard time with only a couple layers of denim, I thought a car door and multiple sheets of thick sheet rock would be overkill. We witnessed first hand the ferocious truth that is hidden inside these shiny light weight cartridges.</p> <p style="font-size: 100%; text-align: left;">We conducted the test as followed: One shot at the door with each of the calibers, tracking each shot and seeing how each caliber performed. First the Keltec shooting the .380, then the Nano with the 9mm, the Sig 229 with the .40 S&amp;W and finally the FN FNX with the .45ACP. Each round had no problem being extremely accurate and hitting the door right where I aimed. After the first round of four shots, one from each gun, we walked over to check the results. EVERY SHOT went right through the door, in some cases even hit the steel support beam inside the door, and exited the other side with no problem at all. When we pulled back the Door, we saw the same thing happen to the dry wall, every single round penetrated the door, the particle board, the sheet metal and the 3/4” drywall behind it with ease.</p> <p>After seeing how easily the ammo penetrated all the barriers we setup, we decided to stack all the barriers one by one next to each other for the last four shots. We shot the same four rounds and saw the same results. The 9mm, .40cal and .45 had the most penetration going through every barrier we put up. The .380 was the only round that stopped after the door, 3/4” dry wall, the particle board, the sheet metal and then finally came to a stop in the fifth layer of 3/4” drywall.</p> <p><a href="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/laydown.jpg" data-rel="colorbox"><img class="aligncenter size-large wp-image-2710" src="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/laydown.jpg?resize=500%2C166" alt="liberty-civil-defense-ammo" srcset="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/laydown.jpg?resize=500%2C166 500w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/laydown.jpg?resize=200%2C66 200w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/laydown.jpg?resize=100%2C33 100w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/laydown.jpg?resize=150%2C50 150w" sizes="(max-width: 500px) 100vw, 500px" data-recalc-dims="1"></a></p> <p style="font-size: 100%; text-align: left;">Only two of the rounds fragmented and those are the rounds that actually hit the ballistic gel. One of the design characteristics of Liberty is that the projectile remains intact while shooting through a barrier, door, window, whatever it may be. Once the hollow point hits soft tissue, it fills the tip of the ammo forcing the bullet to expand and break into fragments. These fragments blow up almost like a hand grenade causing about a 4.5” wide area of extreme energy transfer with shrapnel. The remaining bottom portion of the bullet stays as a slug and penetrates about 8-12 inches depending on the caliber and what barrier it travels through.</p> <p style="font-size: 100%; text-align: left;">The closest ammunition that could be compared to the design of the fragmenting around is the RIP G2 pre-fragmented hollow point. If we tested the RIP G2 in the same fashion, the first hard barrier would cause the round to break apart and fragment too early. How effective can you really be with ammo that breaks before reaching its target? The ability to penetrate through hard barriers first and then fragment only upon impact of soft tissue, paired with the speed and light carry weight of the Liberty Civil Defense Ammo round makes this ammo far Superior than any other personal defense round on the market. &nbsp;The fragmentation of this ammunition is what makes it the most deadly ammunition available to the civilian market hence the companies slogan “ONE AND DONE.” One shot anywhere in the torso and this fragmenting bullet more than likely will hit one of the vital organs which is one of the ways death occurs from a gun shot wound to the abdomen.</p> <p style="font-size: 100%; text-align: left;"><a href="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/gelshot.jpg" data-rel="colorbox"><img class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-2709" src="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/gelshot.jpg?resize=282%2C169" alt="liberty-civil-defense-ammo" srcset="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/gelshot.jpg?w=282 282w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/gelshot.jpg?resize=200%2C119 200w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/gelshot.jpg?resize=100%2C59 100w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/gelshot.jpg?resize=150%2C89 150w" sizes="(max-width: 282px) 100vw, 282px" data-recalc-dims="1"></a></p> <p style="font-size: 150%; text-align: center;"><strong>There are a lot of other features that the Liberty Civil Defense Ammo&nbsp;&nbsp;has to offer which makes it the best personal defense ammunition for your everyday carry.</strong></p> <ul> <li><strong>REDUCED CARRY WEIGHT:&nbsp;</strong>If your like me, you carry at least a compact to full size firearm on a daily basis, all day, everyday. After a couple hours of carrying a fully loaded Sig P229 with 17 rounds of regular defense ammo your gun becomes more of an annoyance then it is a comfort. The weight of the firearm has a direct relationship to how long you can carry comfortably for, how often you will actually carry the gun, and allowing the firearm to become another part of your everyday wardrobe. The weight allows you to stay with the compact or full size firearm we all love, but still keep the weight at a manageable amount.</li> <li><strong>REDUCED RECOIL:</strong> one of the hardest things I try to teach my students when taking their Concealed Carry Class is the ability to take follow up shots, better known as “Double tap” Because the bullet is super light, the perceived recoil of the firearm is cut by about 30%. This helps you stay on target while taking multiple shots.</li> <li><strong>REDUCED OVER PENETRATION:</strong> The fragmenting ammo ensures that once that bullet hits its intended target, it will not come out the other side. Some high velocity FMJ have the ability to enter and exit the back side of your target, endangering whoever happens to be behind your target. The fragmentation width is about 4.5” inches wide while the base of the ammo penetrates about 12” inches.</li> <li><strong>3X&nbsp;TERMINAL EFFECT:</strong> simply put, more knock down power. I want to be able to stop my attacker in his or her tracks immediately and no matter what. If my attacker is on Crystal Meth and in an adrenaline fueled rage a .380 shot from a 2″ barrel isn’t going to stop him. I want to literally knock him off his feet and put him down on the ground. The Liberty Civil Defense Ammo gives you that knock down power.</li> <li><strong>2X VELOCITY:</strong> Liberty Civil Defense Ammo is about twice as fast as the best hollow point on the market. Speed x Mass = Momentum which delivers the Terminal effect or how the projectile acts once it hits its target. Because the ammo is twice as fast, it delivers much more kinetic energy than a slower heavier round. The more energy being transferred the more damage will be done to the target. The larger caliber rounds will actually throw the target back like you see in the movies. Although the over penetration is reduced because of the deep cavity hollow point design, because of the speed it has been tested and proven that it will penetrate all different types of barriers such as what we tested today: Automotive Glass / Windshield, Car doors, Dry Wall or Plywood, and also most important Heavy Clothing such as denim, leather jackets and sweatshirts.</li> <li><strong><span style="text-decoration: underline;">MADE IN THE USA:</span></strong>&nbsp;Lead Free Projectile made here right in our own back yard, Sarasota Florida from a Monolithic Copper and then Nickel Plated to give it that beautiful shiny aluminum look that is safe to handle and wont go bad.</li> </ul> <p>&nbsp;</p> <h3 style="font-size: 150%; text-align: center;"><strong>So, Should I Buy This Liberty Civil Defense Ammo or not?</strong><br> <strong>YES!</strong></h3> <p style="font-size: 100%; text-align: left;">Based on the findings of my experiment and the science behind the Liberty Civil Defense Ammo, my conclusion is that Liberty Civil Defense Ammo makes some of the best personal defense ammo on the market. Its right up there with Hornady and Speer in my book. I did find an interesting test conducted online that took two six pound roast beef loins and shot each with one round of each bullet. The first with Liberty Civil Defense Ammo and the other&nbsp;a Hornady XTP 147 grain round . The difference in damage to the meat was quite dramatic. The Liberty Civil Defense Ammo&nbsp;caused <strong>massive damage</strong> through the meat, while the XTP punched through the meat with a comparatively small wound track.</p> <p style="font-size: 100%; text-align: left;">I carry this ammo on a daily basis&nbsp;and absolutely love it. The weight makes you forget that your even carrying a firearm at all. In a situation where I &nbsp;had to use my firearm to protect my life, you better believe the Liberty Civil Defense Ammo is and will remain the first choice of me, my family, and my customers for daily carry inside and outside the home, as well as inside the gun shop as well.&nbsp;This ammo is designed to work every single time you pull the trigger, and whoever is on the receiving end of that bullet doesn’t have a chance because of the&nbsp;4.5” wide terminal shock and shrapnel which will put down anyone&nbsp;in the world with one shot. Stock up on as much of this ammunition as you can, it doesn’t go bad and the performance is by far the most impressive personal defense ammunition available to civilians I have come across.</p> <p style="font-size: 100%; text-align: left;"><a href="http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/meat-shot.jpg" data-rel="colorbox"><img class="aligncenter wp-image-2718 size-large" src="http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/meat-shot.jpg?resize=500%2C400" alt="liberty-civil-defense-ammo" srcset="http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/meat-shot.jpg?resize=500%2C400 500w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/meat-shot.jpg?resize=187%2C150 187w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/meat-shot.jpg?resize=100%2C80 100w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/meat-shot.jpg?resize=150%2C120 150w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/meat-shot.jpg?w=1600 1600w" sizes="(max-width: 500px) 100vw, 500px" data-recalc-dims="1"></a></p> <p style="font-size: 100%; text-align: left;">Prices fluctuate from place to place, and most of these ammunition websites will trick you into thinking your getting a great deal on a box of ammo for $18, but when you go to check out they add $15 in shipping and handling, which most people don’t realize. &nbsp;I recommend if you want to save money, place an order&nbsp;with us&nbsp;on <a title="Florida Gun Classifieds - Ammo For Sale" href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/liberty-civil-defense-ammo/">FloridaGunClassifieds.com</a>. Classifieds – Gun Giveaway Contest" href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/gun-giveaway-contest/"><span style="color: #3b5998;">GUN GIVEAWAY</span></a></b>&nbsp;contest.</p> <p style="text-align: center;">Travis from Orlando is our Gun Giveaway Contest Winner 2014! A brand new Springfield XDS .45ACP!</p> <p style="text-align: left;"><a href="http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/05/Travis.jpg" data-rel="colorbox"><img be conducting another&nbsp;<b><a title="Florida Gun Classifieds – Gun Giveaway Contest" href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/gun-giveaway-contest/"><span style="color: #3b5998;">GUN GIVEAWAY</span></a>&nbsp;</b>every six months so keep sharing, liking and promoting Florida Gun Classifieds!</p> <p><strong>Florida Gun Classifieds</strong>&nbsp;is conducting a&nbsp;<b><a title="Florida Gun Classifieds – Gun Giveaway Contest" href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/gun-giveaway-contest/"><span style="color: #3b5998;">GUN GIVEAWAY</span></a>&nbsp;</b>which will of&nbsp;<strong>Florida Gun Classifieds</strong>, Matt Adika.<strong>&nbsp;Florida Gun Classifieds</strong>&nbsp;will be promoting this contest throughout the end of the year on its Facebook, Twitter and Instagram accounts.</p> <p>We are creating a community of active firearms enthusiasts, which will allow us to provide our community with direct access to our&nbsp;<strong>n</strong><strong>ew guns for sale&nbsp;</strong>and&nbsp;<strong>u</strong><strong>sed guns for sale</strong>, as well as a huge community of knowledge and resources. “These campaigns were all about creating a local community of gun lovers and anyone who supports our 2nd Amendment rights, freedom and the Constitution” said Adika. “Our goal is for this site to be interactive, informative and a destination that our community bookmarks and visits first whenever they are looking to&nbsp;<strong>buy used guns for sale&nbsp;</strong>or post&nbsp;<b>used guns for sale.</b></p> <p><b>Florida Gun Classifieds</b>&nbsp;is also in the process of creating a Firearms Forum where the community can discuss issues ranging from “What is the best concealed carry gun?” to “What ammo would you recommend for personal defense?” and other issues regarding the gun community and our rights as Americans. “I wanted a marketing campaign that actually had excitement behind it. href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/laser-ammo-laser-firearm-training/" title="Laser Ammo – Indoor Laser Firearm Training System">Laser Ammo – Indoor Laser Firearm Training System</a></h3> <p class="meta dotted"><span class="dashicons-before user"><a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/author/matt-adika/" title="Posts by Matt Adika" rel="author">Matt Adika</a></span> <span class="dashicons-before folderb"><a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/category/firearms-blog/" rel="category tag">Firearms Blog</a></span> <span class="dashicons-before clock"><span>January 12, 2015</span></span></p> <div class="entry-content"> <img width="150" height="66" src="http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/laserammo_main_1.jpg?fit=150%2C66" class="attachment-blog-thumbnail size-blog-thumbnail wp-post-image" alt="laser-firearm-training" srcset="http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/laserammo_main_1.jpg?w=796 796w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/laserammo_main_1.jpg?resize=200%2C88 200w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/laserammo_main_1.jpg?resize=500%2C222 500w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/laserammo_main_1.jpg?resize=100%2C44 100w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/laserammo_main_1.jpg?resize=150%2C66 150w" sizes="(max-width: 150px) 100vw, 150px"> <h1 style="font-size: 200%; text-align: center;"><strong>Laser Ammo Laser Firearm Training System</strong></h1> <p style="font-size: 125%; text-align: center;"><a href="http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/laserammo_main_1.jpg" data-rel="colorbox"><img class="aligncenter size-large wp-image-2234" src="http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/laserammo_main_1.jpg?resize=500%2C222" alt="laser-firearm-training" srcset="http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/laserammo_main_1.jpg?resize=500%2C222 500w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/laserammo_main_1.jpg?resize=200%2C88 200w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/laserammo_main_1.jpg?resize=100%2C44 100w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/laserammo_main_1.jpg?resize=150%2C66 150w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/laserammo_main_1.jpg?w=796 796w" sizes="(max-width: 500px) 100vw, 500px" data-recalc-dims="1"></a></p> <p style="font-size: 125%; text-align: center;">There are three different options from Laser Ammo for their indoor range products. They vary in ability and price, but each one is great in their own way.</p> <h2 style="font-size: 200%; text-align: center;"><strong>MY HOME RANGE Indoor Laser Firearm Training Range System</strong></h2> <p style="font-size: 150%; text-align: center;"><strong>Price: $300</strong></p> <div style="width: 500px; " class="wp-video"><span class="mejs-offscreen">Video Player</span><div id="mep_1" class="mejs-container svg wp-video-shortcode mejs-video" tabindex="0" role="application" aria-label="Video Player" style="width: 500px; height: 281px;"><div class="mejs-inner"><div class="mejs-mediaelement"><div class="me-cannotplay"><a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/My-home-range-paper-2.mp4?_=2"><span>Download File</span></a></div><video class="wp-video-shortcode" id="video-2233-2" width="500" height="281" preload="metadata" style="width: 100%; height: 100%; display: none;"><source type="video/mp4" src="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/My-home-range-paper-2.mp4?_=2"><a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/My-home-range-paper-2.mp4">http://floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/My-home-range-paper-2.mp4</a></video></div><div class="mejs-layers"></div><div class="mejs-controls" style="display: none;"></div><div class="mejs-clear"></div></div></div></div> <p style="font-size: 100%; text-align: left;">My Home Range is an indoor laser firearm training system that allows you to use a laser cartridge in your REAL firearm and shoot paper targets on a wall or any surface that the laser can hit and be seen by any webcam. The laser firearm training system comes with one multi-cailber laser cartridge that can be used in 9mm, .40 cal or .45 caliber guns and the software needed to track the shots being fired. The software allows you to use paper targets, point the webcam at the target then you select on the program up to 9 different target areas. When the software sees the laser beam hit the target area it records the hit so you can see in real time your accuracy. There are different modes in the laser firearm training such as the system actively calling out which target to shoot and you have to hit the target it calls. It will record your reaction time, accuracy etc. They have other calibers available individually like .38 special, .380, 9×18, and even a hunting package that has shotgun calibers like 12GA, 20GA, .308 and 30-06. Individual cartridges run around $130. They sell revolver .38 special pro packs that have either five or six cartridges to fill the entire cylinder so you can keep shooting over and over simulating a real life shooting using the &nbsp;laser firearm training, and also give you a discount for purchasing multiple cartridges in one package.</p> <ul> <li>revolver pro pack (5) cartridges run $460</li> <li>revolver pro pack (6) cartridges run $550</li> </ul> <p>CHECK OUT THE DEMO VIDEO: <a title="Laser Ammo - My Home Range Laser Firearm Training System" href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=fvdCA_LdMV4">Laser Ammo My Home Range Laser Firearm Training Demo</a></p> <ol> <li>PRICE: $175 for the same multi-caliber pistol cartridge alone.</li> <li>PRICE: $200 for the multi-caliber pistol cartridge and .223 cartridge adapter</li> </ol> <p style="font-size: 125%; text-align: center;"><b>TOTAL PRICE: $300</b> for the SureStrike LASR range software and multi-caliber pistol cartridge</p> <h3 style="font-size: 200%; text-align: center; line-height: 1.5;"><strong>SMOKELESS RANGE HOME LASER FIREARM TRAINING SIMULATOR</strong></h3> <p style="font-size: 200%; text-align: center; line-height: 1;"><strong>Price $600</strong></p> <div style="width: 500px; " class="wp-video"><span class="mejs-offscreen">Video Player</span><div id="mep_2" class="mejs-container svg wp-video-shortcode mejs-video" tabindex="0" role="application" aria-label="Video Player" style="width: 500px; height: 281px;"><div class="mejs-inner"><div class="mejs-mediaelement"><div class="me-cannotplay"><a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/Laser-ammo-interactive.mp4?_=3"><span>Download File</span></a></div><video class="wp-video-shortcode" id="video-2233-3" width="500" height="281" preload="metadata" style="width: 100%; height: 100%; display: none;"><source type="video/mp4" src="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/Laser-ammo-interactive.mp4?_=3"><a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/Laser-ammo-interactive.mp4">http://floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/Laser-ammo-interactive.mp4</a></video></div><div class="mejs-layers"></div><div class="mejs-controls" style="display: none;"></div><div class="mejs-clear"></div></div></div></div> <p style="font-size: 100%; text-align: left;">The smokeless range home laser firearm training simulator is shooting simulator that allows you to use a laser cartridge in your REAL firearm and shoot interactive targets on either a TV or Projector. There are currently 15 different shooting modes and games that simulate drills, moving targets, trap and skeet, timed drills, accuracy drills, the size, speed and number of the targets can be adjusted to simulate distance. There also multiplayer modes where each person can battle each other with games like target flip in which you have six “swinging metal targets” mounted vertically on a pole, so when the right player hits the target on the right, it swings over to the left and the goal is to get all your targets on your friends side before he shoots back and hits his target to bring it back to your side. Once the laser firearm training cartridge is installed, you can use the trigger and laser to act like you mouse to operate the program, so there is no need to have to leave your shooting position. They recommend if you have a projector to use it, but I am going to set it up on my 70″ LED TV. There should be no problem unless there is a lot of glare on the screen. You can always add an anti glare screen film to solve this problem.</p> <p style="font-size: 100%; text-align: left;">Like My Home Range, a webcam will be pointed at the TV or projection to record where the laser hits, and the software is so advanced it allows you to an interactive fun experience that is unlike anything you’ve experienced.</p> <p>WATCH THE VIDEO DEMO: <a title="Laser Ammo - Smokeless Range Laser Firearm Training System" href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=dfp6Hasi0Gc">https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=dfp6Hasi0Gc</a></p> <p style="font-size: 100%; text-align: left;">They have other calibers available in the laser firearm training system that can be purchased individually like .38 special, .380, .223 and even a hunting package that has shotgun calibers like 12GA, 20GA, .308 and 30-06. Individual cartriges run around $130. They sell revolver .38 special pro packs that have either five or six cartridges to fill the entire cylinder so you can keep shooting over and over simulating a real life shooting, and also give you a discount for purchasing multiple cartridges in one package.</p> <ul> <li>individual cartridges retail between $130-$160 depending on caliber</li> <li>revolver pro pack (5) cartriges retail for $460</li> <li>revolver pro pack (6) cartriges retail for $550</li> </ul> <ol> <li>PRICE: $350 for the laser firearm training simulator software</li> <li>PRICE: $175 for the same multi-caliber pistol cartridge (x2 for multiplayer)</li> </ol> <p style="font-size: 125%; text-align: center;"><b>TOTAL PRICE: $575-600</b> for a one pistol or rifle setup</p> <h4 style="font-size: 200%; text-align: center; line-height: 1.5;"><strong>LaserPET™&nbsp;ELECTRONIC TARGET </strong></h4> <p style="font-size: 150%; text-align: center;"><strong>LASER FIREARM TRAINING</strong></p> <p style="font-size: 150%; text-align: center;"><strong>$125-$325</strong></p> <p style="font-size: 100%; text-align: left;">The last option is a stand alone electronic laser firearm training target called the LaserPET™ and has three basic modes of operation.</p> <ol> <li>Target Mode: In this mode, the LaserPET™ simply lets you know whether you hit the target or not. You can use the full screen as the target area, or you can use one of the provided inserts to further refine and reduce the target area to require a more accurate shot.</li> <li>2. Timed Mode: Timed mode gives you a start signal, then records the amount of time it takes you to fire an accurate shot on the target. It’s excellent for simulating the pressure of competition, which is the closest you can get to the stress of self-defense. The best part is that you’ll KNOW you are getting better as you see your times drop. In this mode, the possibilities for training are only limited by your imagination. You can place the gun anywhere you want, whether it’s in a holster, on a nightstand, or locked away for safety. You can then position the LaserPET™ target anywhere you wish to simulate the place you expect a threat or to test a specific skill. The LaserPET™ gives you a start signal and then shows you how long it takes you to fire an accurate shot.</li> <li>3. Speed Mode: In this environment, the LaserPET™ records how many accurate shots you can fire in 5 seconds. It could be used for reload drills, movement drills, or anything else you can think of. Again, the possibilities are only limited by your imagination.</li> </ol> <p style="font-size: 100%; text-align: left;">These are nice and a very affordable option to allows you to practice and conduct drills that you normally would not or could not do with live ammunition. You can put the laserPET laser firearm training in different locations around your house and practice with your REAL gun simulating different scenarios inside your home such as clearing rooms, different shooting positions and distances and taking cover while firing. You’ll be surprised how difficult it really is to hit a target 25 feet away from you in your own home. Now imagine that target is a home invader that’s moving or running toward you.</p> <p><a title="LaserPET Electronic Target Laser Firearm Training Target" href="http://youtu.be/YI8xc6Im7hw">WATCH THE LaserPET™&nbsp;ELECTRONIC TARGET VIDEO DEMO</a><br> <a title="LaserPET T Electronic Target Laser Firearm Training Features" href="http://youtu.be/VNg14BQ-8LM">WATCH THE FEATURE DESCRIPTION</a></p> <ol> <li>PRICE: $125 for a single unit</li> <li>PRICE: $325 for a three pack</li> <li>PRICE: $175 for the multi-caliber pistol cartridge</li> <li>+ADD $25 for .223 adapter</li> </ol> <p style="font-size: 125%; text-align: center;"><b>TOTAL PRICE: $300</b> for one unit with the multi-caliber pistol cartridge</p> <p style="font-size: 125%; text-align: center;"><b>TOTAL PRICE: $500</b> for three units with multi-caliber pistol cartridge</p> <h5 style="font-size: 150%; text-align: center; line-height: 1;"><strong>OPTIONAL ADD-ON FEATURES TO ANY OF THE THREE LASER AMMO LASER FIREARM&nbsp;TRAINING SYSTEM</strong></h5> <p>If you own a Glock pistol and want to use your own handgun, They sell a automatic reset trigger that you can install into your handgun so you do not have the rack the slide after each shot. Great for training on your own Glock pistol.</p> <ol> <li><strong>PRICE: $200</strong></li> </ol> <h6 style="font-size: 150%; text-align: center; line-height: 1;"><strong>OPTIONAL AIRSOFT CONVERSION KITS FOR LASER AMMO LASER TRAINING SYSTEM</strong></h6> <p>Instead of using a REAL pistol or rifle to practice, the&nbsp;laser firearm training has adapters and conversion kits for airsoft pistols and rifles. The vibration from the recoil from the airsoft gun triggers the vibration sensitive cartridge which shoots the laser. This setup is as close to real life training drills as you can get because of the recoil of the airsoft gun. This option is awesome and can be used by instructors to teach students without ever firing a live round. This laser firearm training can be used to teach anyone how to shoot without any risk involved. There are many instructors that use this simulation along with the airsoft setup with their students. It’s obvious Laser Ammo listens to their&nbsp;client’s needs, pride themselves as bringing the best and most innovative training products they&nbsp;develop. They do have a few different solutions for Airsoft users for both for pistols and rifles. The laser firearm training system is not a substitution for live fire practice, but definitely the closest you can come.</p> <p style="font-weight: lighter;"><strong>The advantages of training with Airsoft:</strong></p> <ol style="font-weight: lighter;"> <li>Safe and relatively inexpensive</li> <li>Ability to train on real scenarios / realistic drills</li> <li>Full blowback and no need to recycle the gun</li> <li>Look and feel of your favorite firearms</li> <li>Can train anywhere – indoors and outdoors</li> <li>No need of special license.</li> <li>Can be used with war-gaming and close quarter battles</li> <li>Develop your combat skills, by training force-on-force with different teams.</li> <li>Train outdoors with friends.</li> </ol> <p><strong>The advantages of using Lasers in conjunction with Airsoft are:</strong></p> <ol style="font-weight: lighter;"> <li>Train with simulators, electronic targets, and tactical vests like laser tag vests or even military MILES gear.</li> <li>Get full blowback when training with your LaserPET™ / L.A.S.R software.</li> <li>No need to cycle the handle on your AR 15.</li> <li>Train safely with your friends</li> <li>Easy to install</li> <li>Practice combat training and more realistic scenarios at home or outdoors.</li> </ol> <p>Changing your Airsoft to a laser-emitting weapon has never been so easy with the SureStrike™ adapters.</p> <p>*If you do not already own an airsoft pistol or rifle, you do need to purchase one.</p> <ul> <li>The average price for the KWA ATP is about $150</li> <li>Airsoft rifles start at about $50</li> </ul> <ol> <li style="font-size: 125%;">AIRSOFT PISTOL SYSTEM&nbsp;w/ simulator</li> </ol> <ul> <li>PRICE: $150-175 for the KWA airsoft pistol</li> <li>PRICE: $200 for the airsoft pistol conversion kit for KWA ATP</li> <li>PRICE: $125 for the vibration sensitive laser cartridge</li> </ul> <p style="font-size: 125%; text-align: center;"><strong>TOTAL PRICE $325</strong> TO CONVERT AIRSOFT PISTOL</p> <p style="font-size: 125%; text-align: center;"><strong>TOTAL PRICE $475</strong> TO BUY AND CONVERT AIRSOFT PISTOL:</p> <ol start="2"> <li style="font-size: 125%;">AIRSOFT RIFLE SYSTEM&nbsp;w/ simulator</li> </ol> <ul> <li>PRICE: $50-100</li> <li>PRICE: $75 for the rifle adapter which goes into the barrel of the rifle.</li> <li>PRICE: $125 for the vibration sensitive laser cartridge</li> </ul> <p style="font-size: 125%; text-align: center;"><strong>TOTAL PRICE $250</strong> TO CONVERT AIRSOFT RIFLE</p> <p style="font-size: 150%; text-align: center;">TO ORDER OR FOR MORE INFORMATION CONTACT US TODAY!</p> <p style="font-size: 150%; tag-gun-practice tag-snap-caps tag-training-ammo" id="post-2214"> <div class="shadowblock"> <div class="dashicons-before comment-bubble"><a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/snap-caps/#respond" class="bubble cp-fixed-color">0</a></div> <h3 class="loop"><a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/snap-caps/" title="What are Snap Caps?">What are Snap Caps?</a></h3> <p class="meta dotted"><span class="dashicons-before user"><a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/author/matt-adika/" title="Posts by Matt Adika" rel="author">Matt Adika</a></span> <span class="dashicons-before folderb"><a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/category/firearms-blog/" rel="category tag">Firearms Blog</a></span> <span class="dashicons-before clock"><span>January 12, 2015</span></span></p> <div class="entry-content"> <img width="150" height="98" src="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/snap-caps.jpg?fit=150%2C98" class="attachment-blog-thumbnail size-blog-thumbnail wp-post-image" alt="what-are-Snap-Caps" srcset="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/snap-caps.jpg?w=365 365w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/snap-caps.jpg?resize=200%2C131 200w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/snap-caps.jpg?resize=100%2C65 100w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/snap-caps.jpg?resize=150%2C98 150w" sizes="(max-width: 150px) 100vw, 150px"> <h1 style="font-size: 200%; text-align: center;"><strong>What are Snap Caps?</strong></h1> <p></p> <p style="font-size: 125%; text-align: center;">Snap Caps are actually a brand name, but they have become the moniker for dummy rounds.</p> <p style="font-size: 150%; text-align: center;"><a href="http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/snapcaps-detail.gif" data-rel="colorbox"><img class="alignnone wp-image-2220 size-full" src="http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/snapcaps-detail.gif?resize=443%2C237" alt="what-are-snap-caps" data-recalc-dims="1"></a></p> <p>Snap caps come as solid plastic trainers, there are hollow plastic ones with brass ends and spring loaded primers for you firing pin to hit, there are also solid aluminum ones. The aluminum ones are my favorite, as they last the longest. Florida Gun Classifieds carries all the common calibers for sale in our store and online. We use them in our NRA basic pistol shooting course and our concealed weapons permit classes to train our students before they ever fire a live round. we discuss how to identify ammo calibers and the difference between rimfire and center-fire cartridges. I personally have the A-Zoom aluminum snap caps in 9mm, .40 S&amp;W, .45 ACP, and .223 for my own personal training drills.<br> </p> <h3 style="font-size: 140%; text-align: left;"><strong>What are Snap Caps used for?</strong></h3> <p></p> <ul type="square"> <li>They were made to save the firing pin in your gun from degradation due to dry firing on an empty chamber. But they have more uses than just that. Here is some ideas you can use to help you, safely, learn how to operate you gun, and be a more proficient shooter. They are modeled and scaled exactly to the same dimensions as the cartridge (read bullet) for you gun. So you can load them in your magazine, just like loading live rounds. This may seem silly to some, but everyone has to do it a first time.</li> <li>You can practice racking your slide without it locking back, when you have a magazine inserted.</li> <li>Malfunction drills: There are 3 types of malfunctions in a semi automatic: With Snap Caps, you can simulate all these types of malfunctions and practice clearing them all.</li> </ul> <p></p> <h3 style="font-size: 140%; text-align: left;"><strong>What Types of Malfunctions can you simulate with Snap Caps?</strong></h3> <p></p> <ol> <li>Type 1: Failure to Fire – This is pretty simple to spot. You pull the trigger and nothing happens. Click and no bang! When this happens, you should wait about 30 seconds, then smack your magazine to make sure it’s seated in your pistol, and rack your slide. Known as tap and rack.</li> <li>Type 2: Failure to eject – often called a stovepipe. The spent casing will be sticking out of your ejection port like a stove pipe sticking out of a roof. Simply rack your slide, hard, and continue. If this happens often, you should start investigating as to why.</li> <li>Type 3: Feed Way Stoppage- This type of malfunction can even give experienced shooters a major concern. Sometimes called a “double feed” or “failure to extract” a feed way stoppage happens when two cartridges are in the firing chamber at one time. What happens is The ‘spent’ cartridge you just fired was not successfully ejected from the firing chamber and then another cartridge was pushed into the breech. Because more than one cartridge was forced into the chamber the firearm is now rendered unusable. Feed way malfunctions are usually NOT a quick fix like a stove pipe.</li> </ol> <h4 style="font-size: 160%; text-align: center;">The rule of thumb is to lock, rip, clear, then rack 3 times and reload.</h4> <p>Rip means to get a firm grip on your magazine while pressing the mag release button, and rip the magazine from the weapon. While it is out try to lock your slide back. If it won’t move, you’re going to have to get physical with it. Once the rounds are clear, reload with a new magazine, and continue shooting. This is going to cost you time, and there is no simple fix, This is just the best way I’ve found to deal with it. If you’re in a bad situation, you may have to find “other means” of fighting. Read up on those malfunctions or watch hundred of videos online.</p> <p style="font-size: 100%; text-align: left;">Another great thing to do with snap caps is “flinch control” or “recoil anticipation” control. Have you ever been to the range and you feel like you’re doing everything right? Right grip, stance, breathing, etc… But you are still shooting low and left. You’re probably anticipating recoil. All shooters suffer from this, it’s just happens, and it’s something you have to work on. When you go to the range randomly place snap caps in your magazines, mixed with live rounds. When you go to fire the pistol and it’s a snap cap, you’ll notice right away if you are anticipating. Your muzzle will sharply point to the floor when you pull that trigger. Your mind is unwittingly trying to compensate for the recoil of your weapon. You’ll be surprised how much you really do move. There is no other way to practice this, except get to the range and do this.</p> <h5 style="font-size: 160%; text-align: center;">Spend time at home with the snap caps.</h5> <p style="font-size: 100%; text-align: left;"><a href="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/snap-caps.jpg" data-rel="colorbox"><img class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-2218" src="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/snap-caps.jpg?resize=365%2C240" alt="what-are-Snap-Caps" srcset="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/snap-caps.jpg?w=365 365w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/snap-caps.jpg?resize=200%2C131 200w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/snap-caps.jpg?resize=100%2C65 100w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/snap-caps.jpg?resize=150%2C98 150w" sizes="(max-width: 365px) 100vw, 365px" data-recalc-dims="1"></a></p> <p style="font-size: 500%; text-align: center;"><b>BUT REMEMBER!</b></p> <p style="font-size: 150%; text-align: center;"><b>REMOVE ALL LIVE AMMUNITION FROM THE ROOM BEFORE STARTING DRY FIRE PRACTICE!</b></p> <p>Not just your weapon. Physically take it into another room. Then load a magazine with snap caps, work on all the drills I mentioned here, If you have a laser for your pistol, put it on there and watch what your muzzle is doing. Once you can keep that barrel still, then go to the range and practice with a mix of live rounds and Snap Caps, as I suggested before. I guarantee, you’ll be a better shooter in no time.</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p></p><center>Special thanks to&nbsp;“The Beretta Guy” for this great article!</center><p></p> <div class="sharedaddy id="post-1772"> <div class="shadowblock"> <div class="dashicons-before comment-bubble"><a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/gun-safety-rules/#respond" class="bubble cp-fixed-color">0</a></div> <h3 class="loop"><a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/gun-safety-rules/" title="Gun Safety Rules – Ten Basic Gun Safety Rules for Safe Firearms Use">Gun Safety Rules – Ten Basic Gun Safety Rules for Safe Firearms Use</a></h3> <p class="meta dotted"><span class="dashicons-before user"><a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/author/matt-adika/" title="Posts by Matt Adika" rel="author">Matt Adika</a></span> <span class="dashicons-before folderb"><a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/category/firearms-blog/" rel="category tag">Firearms Blog</a></span> <span class="dashicons-before clock"><span>December 6, 2014</span></span></p> <div class="entry-content"> <img width="150" height="113" src="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/12/gun-safety-rules.png?fit=150%2C113" class="attachment-blog-thumbnail size-blog-thumbnail wp-post-image" alt="gun-safety-rules" srcset="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/12/gun-safety-rules.png?w=258 258w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/12/gun-safety-rules.png?resize=197%2C150 197w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/12/gun-safety-rules.png?resize=100%2C75 100w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/12/gun-safety-rules.png?resize=150%2C113 150w" sizes="(max-width: 150px) 100vw, 150px"> <h2>Guns are used safely millions upon millions of times every year, and each gun has the potential to kill or do serious bodily injury. &nbsp;Any individual that owns a firearm needs to learn Gun Safety Rules which are the basic foundation for the knowledge, skills and attitude necessary for owning a firearm. Gun Safety Rules protect ourselves and others around us, we need to follow Gun Safety Rules at all times when handling any type of firearm, including&nbsp;handguns like revolvers and pistols, rifles, shotguns, muzzle-loaders, and even airguns.</h2> <section class="list-unit group" style="color: #191919;"> <div class="expert-content-text"> <h3 class="item-heading" style="color: inherit;">1 . <strong>Always</strong> Point a Gun in a Safe Direction.</h3> <p>The most important Gun Safety Rules&nbsp;should be self-explanatory. It is the easiest and most important rule of all gun safety. Another way to say it, aim the gun in the direction that if the gun were to discharge, no injury or property damage will occur.</p> </div> </section> <section class="list-unit group" style="color: #191919;"> <div class="expert-content-text"> <h3 class="item-heading" style="color: inherit;">2. &nbsp;Always Keep Your Gun Unloaded Until Your Ready To Use It.</h3> <p>Most people misinterpret Gun Safety Rules, and ask me “what am I going to do ask the bad guy to please hold on while I load my firearm?” This is not what we say when we say “until your ready to use.” When I get dressed in the morning and put my belt and holster on, and put that firearm in my holster, at that point its READY TO USE. If I have a safe at home and the gun is locked in the safe, IT IS READY TO USE. Now if i’m throwing a super bowl party where my friends are drinking and my gun is in my dresser drawer not locked, IT IS NOT READY TO USE. If i am on my way to the range in the car with my friends and I am loading my gun in the back seat, IT IS NOT READY TO USE. Most hunting accidents happen on the way to the actual hunt because the person loading the gun in the back seat accidentally shoots the person in the front. Bottom line is use common sense. Do not leave a loaded gun somewhere someone can stumble upon it and accidentally shoot themselves accidentally.</p> </div> </section> <section class="list-unit group" style="color: #191919;"> <div class="expert-content-text"> <h3 class="item-heading" style="color: inherit;">3 .&nbsp;Always&nbsp;Keep Your Finger off the Trigger.</h3> <p>Gun Safety Rules should be a habit that become&nbsp;second nature and has to be done EVERYTIME you handle a firearm.&nbsp;This is something that many people do not do and I see too often. Some idiot&nbsp;will have his or her finger on the trigger of a gun they are simply carrying, looking down the sights of, etc. Don’t do it! Your finger should be outside the trigger guard on the frame until your ready to shoot, then after shooting should be moved back outside the trigger guard and back on the frame.</p> <h3 class="item-heading" style="color: inherit;">4 .&nbsp;<strong>Always</strong>&nbsp;Assume That Any Gun, at Any Time, is Loaded.</h3> <p>Any time someone hands you a firearm, the fist thing you should do is check to see if the gun is loaded. Gun Safety Rules especially this one should be done habitually. Even if your best friend tells you its safe, check it anyway! &nbsp;Don’t believe it until you see it for yourself. Better safe than dead. Make it a habit to check no matter what. This should be a common practice every time even if YOU know the gun is loaded. It take a second and can keep you and a loved on alive.</p> </div> </section> <section class="list-unit group" style="color: #191919;"> <div class="expert-content-text"> <h3 class="item-heading" style="color: inherit;">5 . Know What You’re Shooting At And Also What Is Behind That.</h3> <div class="list-unit-expert-content">Your&nbsp;target is whatever you intend to shoot, and should be a conscious decision that is considered carefully. Remember we are shooting projectiles that travel upwards to 200 feet per second, and anything traveling at that speed has the ability to hit the target and continue to go&nbsp;travel through to the other side. This is an&nbsp;extremely important Gun Safety Rules because if you shoot a target where people or animals are somewhere behind it, you could kill someone. Don’t get lax about this. You need to know what you are going to shoot at, what is between you and it, and what is beyond it. Pay attention.</div> </div> </section> <section class="list-unit group" style="color: #191919;"> <div class="expert-content-text"> <h3 class="item-heading" style="color: inherit;">6 . Be Familiar With Your Gun And Never Practice With Live Ammunition.</h3> <div class="list-unit-expert-content">Your firearm is like any tool you own. Take the time to Learn everything about it. The options, features and how it operates. Learn these things before you go shooting for the first time… I recommend to purchase Snap Caps or dummy ammunition at home to load, unload, chamber a round, decock the gun, pull the hammer back, learn the trigger pull in single, double, find out how to disable the gun and clean it. When you step up to the firing line, you should already know how to operate the gun you’ll be shooting.</div> </div> </section> <section class="list-unit group" style="color: #191919;"> <div class="expert-content-text"> <h3 class="item-heading" style="color: inherit;">7 . Don’t Shoot at Hard Surfaces.</h3> <div class="list-unit-expert-content">Some Gun Safety Rules are not so obvious like that Hard bullets that hit hard surfaces tend to bounce or ricochet, even off water. It has a tendency to allow bullets and shotgun shot to ricochet (glance off) and fly off in an unintended direction. Not good. Hard surfaces like metal, rocks, and hard wood can do this too – and they can even send the projectile back to the shooter. Shooting yourself by accident can always be prevented and is not only dangerous, but humiliating.</div> </div> </section> <section class="list-unit group" style="color: #191919;"> <div class="expert-content-text"> <h3 class="item-heading" style="color: inherit;">8 . Don’t Rely on a Safety Mechanism.</h3> <div class="list-unit-expert-content">A safety is a mechanical device and any mechanical device can fail. Not only might the safety fail and allow the gun to discharge, but it can also fail to disengage and if you need to use our firearm your screwed. If you follow the first three Gun Safety Rules&nbsp;ALL THE TIME then there is no reason to even have a safety. Your finger should be your safety.</div> </div> </section> <section class="list-unit group" style="color: #191919;"> <div class="expert-content-text"> <h3 class="item-heading" style="color: inherit;">9 . Use the Right Ammo.</h3> </div> </section> <section class="list-unit group" style="color: #191919;"> <div class="expert-content-text"> <p>Make certain the ammunition you’re using is right for your gun. Don’t assume that you have the correct ammo just because it can be crammed into the gun. The caliber of the ammo needs needs to match the firearms caliber exactly to work with the gun’s design and strength factors. The proper cartridge designation is usually marked on the gun barrel and the head stamp of the round. If you have any doubt, consult the gun’s manufacturer or a qualified gunsmith.<a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/12/gun-safety-rules.png"><br> </a></p> </div> </section> <section class="list-unit group" style="color: #191919;"> <div class="expert-content-text"> <h3 class="item-heading" style="color: inherit;">10 . Pay Attention!</h3> <p>When your adrenaline is pumping and your having gun its easy to get distracted and forget about&nbsp;Gun Safety Rules&nbsp;especially with your friends and family. Make sure you follow all the&nbsp;Gun Safety Rules discussed here today and do not be afraid to call out someone not following the rules even someone you don’t know, especially at gun ranges. It could mean the difference between your life and death.&nbsp;Gun Safety Rules&nbsp;are designed to keep you and others safe, and honestly they most are common sense, but most humans lack this trait when doing something new. even expert gun instructors need reminders here and there. Some people might not want to hear it, but everyone that owns a firearm has a responsibility to know all the&nbsp;Gun Safety Rules&nbsp;and actually follow them.</p> <p>Make sure you check out the article about <a title="What is the best gun for concealed carry?" href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/best-gun-concealed-carry/">Concealed Carry</a> and practice these&nbsp;Gun Safety Rules while carrying as well.</p> <p>Matt Adika</p> </div> </section> <div class="sharedaddy sd-sharing-enabled"><div class="robots-nocontent sd-block sd-social sd-social-icon sd-sharing"><h3 comment-bubble"><a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/how-to-aim-a-gun/#respond" class="bubble cp-fixed-color">0</a></div> <h3 class="loop"><a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/how-to-aim-a-gun/" title="How to aim a gun – Common Myths">How to aim a gun – Common Myths</a></h3> <p class="meta dotted"><span class="dashicons-before user"><a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/author/matt-adika/" title="Posts by Matt Adika" rel="author">Matt Adika</a></span> <span class="dashicons-before folderb"><a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/category/firearms-blog/" rel="category tag">Firearms Blog</a></span> <span class="dashicons-before clock"><span>December 6, 2014</span></span></p> <div class="entry-content"> <img width="150" height="73" src="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/12/image.jpg?fit=150%2C73" class="attachment-blog-thumbnail size-blog-thumbnail wp-post-image" alt="How-to-aim-a-gun" srcset="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/12/image.jpg?w=453 453w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/12/image.jpg?resize=200%2C97 200w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/12/image.jpg?resize=100%2C48 100w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/12/image.jpg?resize=150%2C73 150w" sizes="(max-width: 150px) 100vw, 150px"> <h2>Whenever discussion of pistol sights comes up and how to aim a gun, the question inevitably arises about whether such and such sights hit (Point of Impact or POI) to the point of aim (POA). This can be a somewhat subjective thing, as everyone seems to have different expectations.</h2> <h3>The three images above depict common sight pictures used by shooters and how to aim a gun. The first, a traditional 6 o’clock hold, is the most common how to aim a gun and accepted but is wildly inappropriate for practical shooting of any type. It is a holdover from bullseye shooting, where the distance and target size are known. The only way how to aim a gun is with a known target that could line up on an arbitrary point away from the impact area be depended upon to impact the desired area. In the bullseye context, it is obviously a very precise and visually uncluttered way to align the sights to the target.</h3> <p>In practical shooting (fill in whatever real world application you want, it doesn’t matter) – where target type, distance, size, etc. are unknown – the 6 o’clock hold is impractical and artificial. Use of the 6 o’clock hold is also a common excuse when a particular gun’s sights hit really high. Don’t make excuses, fix the sights.</p> <p>The third image would have been something held over from fans of 3 dot sights, as discussed in my first article of this series. As you can see, the iron sights obscure a good portion of the target. If you are aiming at the 7′ tall B-27 “casual man” qual target at 7 yards, then a bit of the blue man hiding behind the sights is no big deal. Start working on harder targets, whether they be distant or smaller targets up close, and it is a losing proposition. The recommended technique on how to aim a gun is to have a POI at the center of the target when the dots are lined up would necessitate having your impact actually be quite low when using the top line of the sights. This becomes a problem when you actually want to use your sights for a harder shot.</p> <p>Think bigger picture when setting up your sights.The second image is what the top shooters strive for, and your sights should be regulated to allow the bullet holes to appear where the top line of the sight cuts through the target area. I generally set up my guns to hit on POA or no more than about 1″ high at 25 yards. I find it acceptable to be able to see the impacts above the line of sight, but never want the impacts to fall below the line of sight. This setup gives the most versatility, and matching the POA and POI gives you a simple “what you see is what you get” sight picture at any distance on any target.This isn’t one of the articles that ends with “what sight picture do you like?” There is only one correct answer, and it is the same given by all the top shooters in every practical shooting discipline from tactical trainers to USPSA champions.</p> <p>Now get to the range and check your sights!</p> <p>To learn more about techniques regarding concealed carry check out our article on <a title="Video: How to Draw a Gun From a Holster? – One Hand Concealed Carry Draw – Concealed Holster Training Drills" href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/how-to-draw-a-gun-from-a-holster/">How to draw a gun from a hoslter.</a></p>
